"Respawn"
{
	"BaseClass" "ability_datadriven"
	"AbilityTextureName"	"ability_name"
	"AbilityBehavior"	"DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_PASSIVE|DOTA_ABILITY_BEHAVIOR_HIDDEN"

	"OnCreated" //  
	{
		"RunScript" // 
		{
			"ScriptFile"	"scripts/vscripts/main_mode.lua" 
			"Function"	"Respoint"
		}
	}
	
	"OnOwnerDied" //  
	{
		"RunScript" // 
		{
			"ScriptFile"	"scripts/vscripts/main_mode.lua" 
			"Function"	"Respawn"
		}
	}

}
